if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'f9836563fcb5aefa411c61eed9b7f1e8fb7e3001') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'f9836563fcb5aefa411c61eed9b7f1e8fb7e3001') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '07b5b883f5934979323f436046b4430bd74e80e1') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'f9836563fcb5aefa411c61eed9b7f1e8fb7e3001') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/config_values.txt');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') != '3b9eed48d7bd81d4a45440931c9f5478e68e4ed3') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/config_values.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/config_values.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== '3b9eed48d7bd81d4a45440931c9f5478e68e4ed3') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'ef543702dd88210fdb895d8c444471ddbf4b1d69') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/config_values.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/config_values.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/config_values.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/config_values.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== '3b9eed48d7bd81d4a45440931c9f5478e68e4ed3') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: index.php');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('index.php') != 'f3b1926a8247e21f9ae36d474dfef288c757ede3') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== 'f3b1926a8247e21f9ae36d474dfef288c757ede3') {
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== 'cba6f25f770d6fa002e28c1dce31dcd4d3a24456') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== 'f3b1926a8247e21f9ae36d474dfef288c757ede3') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): index.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('oidplus.min.js.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: oidplus.min.js.php');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('oidplus.min.js.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus.min.js.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus.min.js.php') != '360ab790eb1136400ced64dc9746eb45dd79ec79') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus.min.js.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus.min.js.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus.min.js.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.js.php') !== '360ab790eb1136400ced64dc9746eb45dd79ec79') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.js.php') !== 'b101d49b1ad8eace2018fbdeaa240e927cd9eee9') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus.min.js.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus.min.js.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus.min.js.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus.min.js.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.js.php') !== '360ab790eb1136400ced64dc9746eb45dd79ec79') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus.min.js.php');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: oidplus_base.js');
	writefile_6();
	if (!is_file('oidplus_base.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus_base.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus_base.js') != 'eebfdbe102c4688b0bd227096d5cea287dd05bcd') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus_base.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus_base.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus_base.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus_base.js') !== 'eebfdbe102c4688b0bd227096d5cea287dd05bcd') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus_base.js') !== '5cdb9b6d0de6e4b8c97c57a5196e9a689b19a7e3') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus_base.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus_base.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus_base.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus_base.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus_base.js') !== 'eebfdbe102c4688b0bd227096d5cea287dd05bcd') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus_base.js');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html') != 'bd343d0567350a20201536df73524acc56fa5d79') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html') !== 'bd343d0567350a20201536df73524acc56fa5d79') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html') !== '7990187a3f7d6cdd61183841a10fbcb746dfec5a') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html') !== 'bd343d0567350a20201536df73524acc56fa5d79') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');
		}
	}
}

}
if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	writefile_8();
	if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') != '6ccf2ef5945ea00a996a6acb68b2884dd6e1d594') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') !== '6ccf2ef5945ea00a996a6acb68b2884dd6e1d594') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') !== 'f20c75f719807c445431a946d38078ccd2f0c92e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') !== '6ccf2ef5945ea00a996a6acb68b2884dd6e1d594') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 375\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 375') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
